panel.promo_price_sum/panel.promo_days, 0.0)\npanel['discount_pct']=np.where(panel.promo_days>0, np.maximum(0, panel.unit_price-panel.promo_price_mean)/panel.unit_price, sorted(glob.glob('/app/sales_transaction_*.csv')):\n    d=pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['store_id','sales_date','units_sold','revenue','promo_price'])\n    d['promo_line']=(d.promo_price>0).astype('int8')\n    sales.append(d.groupby(['store_id','sales_date']).agg(units=('units_sold','sum'), revenue=('revenue','sum'), promo_lines=('promo_line','sum'), rows=('units_sold','size')).reset_index())\nsales=pd.concat(sales, ignore_index=True)\n# Traffic full store-day grid\ntraffic=[]\nfor f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/store_traffic_*.csv')):\n    traffic.append(pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['store_id','traffic_date','customer_count']))\ntraffic=pd.concat(traffic, ignore_index=True).rename(columns={'traffic_date':'date','customer_count':'traffic'})\npanel=traffic.merge(sales,left_on=['store_id','date'],right_on=['store_id','sales_date'],how='left')\nfor c in ['units','revenue','promo_lines','rows']: panel[c]=panel[c].fillna(0)\npanel['month']=pd.to_datetime(panel.date).dt.month.astype('int8')\npanel['dow']=pd.to_datetime(panel.date).dt.dayofweek.astype('int8')\npanel['date_cat']=panel.date\npanel['log_traffic']=np.log1p(panel.traffic)\npanel['promo_rate']=panel.promo_lines/(panel.rows+1)\nprint('panel',panel.shape,panel.revenue.sum(), flush=True)\n# Fit expected log revenue with store and date fixed effects + traffic/promo\nfeatures=['store_id','date_cat','month','dow','log_traffic','promo_rate']\nX=panel[features]; y=np.log1p(panel.revenue.values)\ncat=['store_id','date_cat','month','dow']; num=['log_traffic','promo_rate']\npre=ColumnTransformer([('cat',OneHotEncoder(handle_unknown='ignore'),cat),('num',StandardScaler(with_mean=False),num)], sparse_threshold=1.0)\npipe=make_pipeline(pre,Ridge(alpha=5.0, solver='lsqr'))\npipe.fit(X,y); pred=pipe.predict(X)\npanel['resid']=y-pred; panel['pred_rev']=np.expm1(pred)\nprint('R2',round(r2_score(y,pred),4),'resid sd',panel.resid.std(), flush=True)\n# Same-day visit residuals. If multiple visits store-date, each gets same residual.\nvd=comp_vis.merge(panel[['store_id','date','resid','revenue','pred_rev','traffic']],on=['store_id','date'],how='left')\n# next windows: for each visit, average residual/revenue over same day + next k days at that store\np2=panel[['store_id','date','resid','revenue','pred_rev']].copy(); p2['dt']=pd.to_datetime(p2.date)\nfor k in [0,1,3,7,14]:\n    if k==0:\n        tmp=vd.copy(); tmp['win_resid']=tmp.resid; tmp['win_ratio']=tmp.revenue/tmp.pred_rev\n    else:\n        # merge by store and date interval, use loop via indexed arrays per store\n        records=[]\n        for sid,gvis in comp_vis.groupby('store_id'):\n            days=p2[p2.store_id==sid].sort_values('dt')\n            vals=days.resid.to_numpy(); rev=days.revenue.to_numpy(); predv=days.pred_rev.to_numpy(); dates=days.dt.to_numpy()\n            # dates are continuous daily, use searchsorted\n            for idx,row in gvis.iterrows():\n                start=np.searchsorted(dates, np.datetime64(row.dt), side='left')\n                end=np.searchsorted(dates, np.datetime64(row.dt + pd.Timedelta(days=k)), side='right')\n                if end>start:\n                    records.append((idx, vals[start:end].mean(), rev[start:end].sum()/predv[start:end].sum()))\n        win=pd.DataFrame(records,columns=['idx','win_resid','win_ratio']).set_index('idx')\n        tmp=comp_vis.join(win, how='left')\n    rep=tmp.groupby('rep_id').agg(mean_resid=('win_resid','mean'), median_resid=('win_resid','median'), ratio=('win_ratio','mean'), n=('win_resid','count')).reset_index()\n    for c in ['mean_resid','ratio']:\n        rep[c+'_z']=(rep[c]-rep[c].mean())/rep[c].std(ddof=1)\n    rep=rep.sort_values('mean_resid')\n    print('\\\\nWINDOW',k,'days')\n    print(rep.head(25).to_string(index=False, formatters={c:'{:.3f}'.format for c in ['mean_resid','median_resid','ratio','mean_resid_z','ratio_z']}), flush=True)\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/store_traffic_*.csv')):\n    d=pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['store_id','traffic_date','customer_count'])\n    d['month']=pd.to_datetime(d.traffic_date).dt.month.astype('int8')\n panel['log_size']=np.log1p(panel.store_size_sqm); panel['promo_rate']=panel.promo_lines/(panel.rows+1)\nfeatures=['month','store_type','location','region','log_size','log_traffic','promo_rate','comp_facings','comp_promo_rate']\nX=panel[features]; np.average(s,weights=panel.loc[s.index,'pred']+1)),actual=('revenue','sum'),pred=('pred','sum')).reset_index().rename(columns={'primary_rep_id':'rep_id'})\nrep_sales['ratio']=rep_sales.actual/rep_sales.pred\nfor c in ['sales_resid','sales_w_resid','ratio']: rep_sales[c+'_z']=(rep_sales[c]-rep_sales[c].mean())/rep_sales[c].std(ddof=1)\n# region peer z/rank for s:(s=='eye_level').mean()),endcap_rate=('endcap_display','mean'),checkout_rate=('checkout_display','mean'),promo_stand_rate=('promo_stand','mean'),pos_rate=('pos_materials','mean'),plano_rate=('planogram_compliance','mean')).reset_index())\ntmp=pd.concat(shelf); rows=[]\nfor rid,g in tmp.groupby('rep_id'):\n    w=g.n.values; row={'rep_id':rid,'shelf_n':w.sum()}\n    for c in
